119 米 14 粽 dûng zòng sticky rice dumpling. (variants: 糉, 糭 dûng zòng).
粽子 dûng-dū zòngzi tetrahedron-shaped (southern) dumpling made of glutinous rice wrapped in bamboo or reed leaves (usually eaten during the Dragon Boat Festival).⁶
豆沙粽子 èo-sä-dûng-dū dòushāzòngzi sticky rice dumpling with (red) bean paste filling.⁶
花生粽 fä-säng-dûng/ huāshēngzòng sticky rice dumpling with peanut and other filling.

肉粽子 ngùk-dûng-dū ròuzòngzi sticky rice dumpling with meat filling.⁶
<台> 粽 dûng/ dûng sticky rice dumpling with minced meat filling.
<台> 白粽 bàk-dûng/ sticky rice dumpling with minced meat filling.

<台> 裹粽 gō-dûng/ to make sticky rice dumplings.
